1b1(rgyud): rdo rje mkha 'gro'i rgyud 'azhugs s+ho// /
2a1(rgyud): rnams na pa
2a2(rgyud): skad du/ rgyud kyi rgyal po chen po chen pa dpal rdo mkha' 'gro nas
2a3(rgyud): bya ba/ bcom ldan 'das thugs rje chen po 'phags pa spyan ras
2b1(rgyud): gzigs dbang phyug la phyag 'tshal lo// mkha' 'gro kun dngos sems dpa' ni// rdo rje mkha'
2b2(rgyud): 'gro bde ba'i mchog/ gsang ba mchog gi dges pa na// thams cad bdag nyid rtag tu bzhugs/
2b3(rgyud): 'di ni rang byung bcom ldan 'das// lhag pa yi ni lha gcig nyid// 'byung gnas sgra tshul nges 'byung
2b4(rgyud): rnams// dam tshig spyod pa'i spyod yul yin// 'jig rten gsum du rnyed dka' ba// thog mar dbus
3a1(rgyud): mthar yang dag gnas// 'dod chags ma yin chags bral min// dbu
3a2(rgyud): mar yang ni mi dmigs so// bud med kun gyi sgyu ma'i rgya// 'di ni gnyis med ye shes mchog/ rnyed
3a3(rgyud): dang bde ba kun mos pas// ngan par spyod pa'ang 'grub par 'gyur// nam mkha' kun tu rgyu grub pas//
3a4(rgyud): mkha' 'gro ma zhes rab tu grags// sna tshogs kun tu phyag rgya ni// sna tshogs kun gyis sdom pa yis/
3b1(rgyud): mkha' 'gro kun dang mnyam sbyor ba// rdo rje mkha' 'gro zhes byar grub// de nyid med sems rnal 'byor pa// lA
3b2(rgyud): la dmigs par byed pa dag/ kun tu gzugs brnyan nyid kyi ni// lus sogs rnal 'byor skye ba med// byang chub
3b3(rgyud): sems chen rnal 'byor gang // rnal 'byor dbang phyug rang nyid gtso// byang chub sems 'di rdo rje ste// sangs rgyas kun
3b4(rgyud): gyi rang bzhin no// 'gro ba'i rtsa lag rang bzhin gyis// sna tshogs g.yog te rnam bzhugs pas// de phyir 'bad pa thams
3b5(rgyud): cad kyis// sna tshogs tshul gyis mchod par bya// bdag nyid sangs rgyas thams cad dang // dpa' bo thams cad nyid yin
4a1(rgyud): te/ rang gi lha yi sbyor ba yis// bdag nyid rab tu bsgrub par bya// 'di yis
4a2(rgyud): sangs rgyas thams cad dang // dpa' bo thams cad nyid dang ni// rdo rje 'dzin pa thams cad du// tshe 'di nyid du 'grub
4a3(rgyud): 'gyur zhes// mkha' 'gro kun dang mnyam sbyor ba'i// rdo rje mkha' 'gro bde ba'i mchog/ rdo rje sems dpa' de
4a4(rgyud): bzhin gshegs// dpal ldan bcom ldan 'das kyi gsungs// thams cad nam mkha'i mtshan nyid de// nam
4a5(rgyud): mkha' la ni mtshan nyid med// khams gsum pa ni ma lus pa'i// 'gro kun sgyu ma lta bu yin// brtan pa dang ni
4b1(rgyud): g.yo ba yi// 'gro ba dmigs su med pa ste// mthong ba dang ni reg pa'i dngos// thams cad sgyu ma ji bzhin no// gang
4b2(rgyud): gis blun po 'ching 'gyur ba// 'dir des mkhas rnams rnam par rol// phyag rgya'i sbyor ba 'di yis ni// sa gsum
4b3(rgyud): ma lus bza' bar bya// gzhan du gal te sbyor ba ni// ma tshang mar me lta bur 'da'// gzugs ni sangs rgyas rnam snang
4b4(rgyud): mdzad// tshor ba rdo rje nyi ma yin// 'du shes pad ma gar dbang ste// 'du byed rdo rje rgyal po yin// rnam shes rdo rje sems
4b5(rgyud): dpa' ste// 'di dag dngos kun rang bzhin ni// rdo rje mkha' 'gro zhes byar grags// yang dag chen po gcig pu'i lha/
4b6(rgyud): bde ba thams cad rab ster ba// sgyu ma thams chen po'i rang bzhin gyis// chags bral chags pa zhes byar bshad//
5a1(rgyud): #sa khams ltung byed ma yin te// de bzhin du khams gsod ma'o// me khams 'gugs byed ma yin te// de bzhin rlung ni
5a2(rgyud): gar dbang ngo // na mkha'i khams ni rgyu mche/ rang nyid 'gro ma zhes byar ba shang // sangs rgyas nga kun dang mnyam sbyor ba// mkha' 'gro ma ni 'bar ba'i mchog/
5a3(rgyud): 'byung ba lnga'i rang bzhin gyis// de bzhin rdo rje gtso bor gnas// mig gnyis gti mug rdo rje bshad// nyan pa zhe sdang rdo rjer brjod// sna ni ser
5a4(rgyud): sna rdo rje ste/ ba ni 'dod chags rdo rjer gsus// lus ni phra dog rdo rje ste// skye mched thams cad mnyam sbyor ba/ rdo rje mkha 'gro bde
5a5(rgyud): ba'i mchogagazugs 'di thams cad stong pa nyid// stong pa'i tshul gyi mig gis ni// dogs pa me par bsgom pa'i mchog
5a6(rgyud): rnam par mi rtog pa yis lnga// na mkha'i tshul gyis sems kyis ni// der ni thams cad na mkha'i dngos// dogs pa med pa'i bsgom pa ldan//
5a7(rgyud): rnam par mi rtog skye 'gyur zhes/ rdo rje sems dpa' de bzhin gshegs/ bcom ldan rdo rje cad kyis gsungs/ de mas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa khams
5b1(rgyud): cad thog pa med cing gdon mi za ba chen po'i dam tshig ces bya ba'i rim ting nge 'dzin la snyoms par zhus nas// 'di skadas ces gsung so// ji srid 'khor ba'i ni/ mkhas
5b2(rgyud): mchog 'dug par gyur pa'i mer/ de srid sems can mtshungs med don// mya ngan mi mnga' bar mdzad// de ltar sems cad dam pa rnams// srid pa'i zhags pa'i
5b3(rgyud): 'jigs med par/ mi skyo bar mi brtson 'grus kyis// rtags tu sems can don rnams mdzad// nam mkha'i gnas kyi mthar thugs par// smon lam rnam par
5b4(rgyud): spyod cing // sems can don brtsom so sam gyis ni// dpa' bo srid pa spyod par mdzad/ rtag tu 'dod pas myos pa yi// lha yi bu 'di rnams dang ni/ gzhan yang skye bo chag
5b5(rgyud): can phyir/ 'dod chags thams cad dag par mdzad/ bde chen shin du grub bya'i phyir/ rtog pa rgyas pa sbyin pa dang / phog mya tha ma med pa'i mchog/ rtog pa thams cad dang por bshad/
5b6(rgyud): 'das pa'i dus na ma sngon byung ba// rtog pa dang po bde ba che/ der ni rdo rje sems can gyis// lhag pa yi ni lha gcig bzhugs// 'jig rten khams rnams mtha' yas kyi/ sems can kun
5b7(rgyud): don 'byung bya'i phyim/ klu dang rob mo sogs pa'i gar// srid pa kun gyi mtsho bor gyur// sems can thams cad 'byung ba yi// dga' ba yang dag bsdus pa yang / de nas sems can skye
5'a1(rgyud): 'gyur ba'i// 'dod pa'i chags pa rnam spangs te/ nges 'dul bar ni mkhyen nasu// yi ge las 'byung rnam spangs shing / namakha'i dakhung bdag med pa/ dag pa nyid du de nas
5'a2(rgyud): son/ de nas sems can sangs rgyas kyi// bla med don ni nus med pa'i/ stong pa nyid la rtag bzhugs pa'i// 'gro kun stong pa bcom nA ni/ thas cad dmyal bar ltung mthong ste// slar yang bdag dang gzhan
5'a3(rgyud): don la/ mos pas gus pa nyis du gyur// de nas 'jig rten khams kun nas// bzhugs pa'i sangs rgyas kun sdus te/ myur ba nyid du bdag la bskul/ oM mahA su kha badz+ra satwa dza hUM baM ho su
5'a4(rgyud): su ra ta tAM/ 'dis ni bskrun pa tsam gyis kyang / dag pa'i bde ba kun ster ba// 'dod pa'i don kun grub byed cing / 'gro kun bde ba bskyed par gyur pa ni 'dod pa'i gzug kyi mchog/ sangs rgyas kun gyis byin
5'a5(rgyud): brlags pa// nga nyid chos kyi sku yi mchog/ sangs rgyas kyi bdag po yin/ sangs rgyas kun gyi sbyor 'phrog cing / sangs rgyas kun gyi bde ba che/ sangs rgyas kun gyi sku chen po/ sangs rgyas kun gyi gsung
5'a6(rgyud): bstan pa/ sangs rgyas kun gyi thugs chen yin// sangs rgyas kun gyi mchod pas che// sangs rgyas kun gyi rgyal po che/ rdo rje 'dzin pa kun bdag/ 'jig rten dbang phyug kun gyi brtso/
5'a7(rgyud): rin chen 'dzin pa kun pa kun gyi dbang // mkha'agro kun dang mnyam sbyor ba// sangs rgyas kum dang mnyam sbyor 'gyur// sangs rgyas kun dang mnyams ra// rdo rje ma'i 'gro zhes byar 'gyu
5'b1(rgyud): dkyil 'khor chen po'i sbyor ba yis/ de nas dkyil 'khor thams cad bri// de yi dbusu tshul bzhin du// rdo rje sems dpa' bzhag par byas/ zla ba'i mdog can 'dzum dang bcas/ 'od za
5'b2(rgyud): dmar po 'khrugs pa las/ sangs rgyas rgyas mdzes pa ste// rgyan kun gyis ni rnam par klubs// zhal bzhi phyag bzhi spyan gsum dang / ral bi'i thor tshugs kyi bcwa brgyan cing / lha mo bzhi da
5'b3(rgyud): yang dag ldan/ sangs rgyas gzugs kyis nye bar brgyan// rtsa zhal zhi zhing g.yas dkar yin// de bzhin gzhan yang g.yon pa dmad/ rgyab zhal ser po gser bsregs 'ad/ thod pa la bzhugs
5'b4(rgyud): gar dang ldan/ sum bcu gsum pa 'jigs par mdzad/ rdo rje dang ni lnga gri dang // dril bu thod pa bsnams pa nyid// mkha' 'gro ma'i 'khor los gang / skyob pa sna tshogs bri bar bya/ mkha' gro kun
5'b5(rgyud): dang mnyam sbyor ba'i// rdo rje mkha'a'agro bde mchog zhes/ rdo rje sems dpa' de bzhin gshegs/ bcom ldan rdo rje can gyis gsungs/ ma dang sring mo bu mo dang / de bzhin nyid du mo rnams ni
5'b6(rgyud): dngos grub thams cad rab bsgrub pas// 'dod pa'i sbyor bas chags par bya/ ba glang rasha dang rta sha sogs/ ngogs pa med pa bza' bya/ 'jig rten la rtag g.yon la spyod/ brtan pa dang ni g.yo ba yi/
5'b7(rgyud): 'gro kun g.yon las byung bas ni/ g.yon gi bza' zhing g.yon mchod bya// pho nya ma gtogs gzhan rnams la/ 'dod barmongs pas bgrod mi bya/ pho nya mo rtag zhen thar par/ 'gyur ba nyid du the mtshem med/
5'b8(rgyud): brtsub pas mchag du 'bang byas ste/ brtul zhugs mi spang brtu la zhubs rdzogs// ngas tshig rim pa spyod pa dang // ca ru'i mtha' ba ldan gcig bya/ rigs lnga pa ni kun spyod pa/
6a1(rgyud): rje mkha' 'gro/ rigs cig nyid du rtag par bya// sbrang ci khrag dang ga bur bcas// tsan dan dmar po sbyar byas la// rdo rje chu dang bsres pa ni// dngos
6a2(rgyud): grub thams cad bsgrub byed pa'i// de dag bdud rtsi lngar ni 'gyur// mthe bong bsrin lag sbyar ba yis// rnal 'byor rig pas rtag tu bza'// zhim pa'i gtung ba
6a3(rgyud): bzhin myangs na// dngos grub rtag pa thob par 'gyur// 'di dag dam tshig dam pa ste// mdzes ma'i gdong can khyod la bshad// las rnams kun la thams bcas
6a4(rgyud): shis// dog pa med par gang spyod kyang // rnam par mi rtag bsgom pa ni// brtul zhugs rnams kyi mchog gi mchog/ las rnams kun la kun du ni// rnam par mi rtog
6a5(rgyud): bsgom byed cing // dogs pa med par kun tu sbyong // de ni dka' thub rnams kyi mchog/ the tshom med pa'i sems kyis ni// skra zla la sogs rjes dngos kyi// yul
6a6(rgyud): rnams ma lus rten byed pa'i// dka' thub shin tu bka' ba'o// gang yang las rnams thams cad la// shes rab dang ni sbyor byas te// de yang stong pa'i gnasu sbyar//
6a7(rgyud): de 'dir bdag chen bka' thub yin// rnam par mi rtog sems kyis ni// shes rab dang ni mtshungs gzugs la// dog med spyad pa'i kun spyod pa'i// de ni bdag tshon
6a8(rgyud): dka' thub yin// shes rab thabs ni ma gtogs par// gang che sems bzhan mi g.yon// de tshe byang chub chen po ni// nges par ster ba nyid bshad// rnam par mi rtog/
6b1(rgyud): rjes 'jug la// rnal 'byor pa ni mngon par brtson// de ni thams cad 'byung ba yi// shes rab pha rol phyin pa yin// gang tshe 'dus byas tshul rnams ni// rnam par mi rtog/
6b2(rgyud): sems kyis su// me long lta bur rab shes pa// de ni shes rab brten pa yin// glog dang chu bur ltar smin pa// gang tshe 'dus byas tshul rnams ni// gang gis ji ltar
6b3(rgyud): mthong 'gyur ga de ni shes rab rten pa yin/ me long nang gi gzugs brnyan dang // rmi lam sgyu ma dri za'i grong // mig 'phrul mtshungs par gang gis mthong // de ni
6b4(rgyud): gtso bo yin par brjod// di ni gang du'ang sngon zhen dang // gang du'ang gnas pa yod ma yin// de ltar yang dag 'byung mod kyi// sgyu ma lta bu'i dngos dag ni// long spyod
6b5(rgyud): khyed 'phag skye 'gyur ba// bde ba yongs su 'gyur bzhing bas// 'bras bu khyad 'phags thob 'gyur ba// ci'i phyir ni 'dod mi bya// brtan g.yo'i dngos po yod min te/
6b6(rgyud): 'on kyang snang ba tsam mtshan nyid// bsgom pa khyad par can gang yin// goms pa'i stobs ni rdzogs pa na// yid 'ong bde ba'i 'brus ni// bla med gsal ba blo yi mthu//
6b7(rgyud): 'bras bu don gnyer rgyu bsgrubs na/ der ni lha mo su zhig 'gog/ de bas 'bad pa thams cad kyis// kun du 'gro ma mchod par bya// bkang thub sdom pa mi zad pas//
6b8(rgyud): lus ni skams shing sdug bsngal 'gyur// sdug bsngal gyis ni sems g.yengs na// g.yengs pas dngos grub gzhan du 'gyur// lus dang sems ni brtan gyur na/
6'a1(rgyud): rdo mala' gro/ #bde ba thams cad brtan par 'gyur/ sdug bsngal gyis ni g.yo gyur pas// shin tu 'gog par 'go par 'gyur// des na lus dang ngag sems rnamam// brtan
6'a2(rgyud): par byas na byang chub thob// gzhan yang dus min 'chi ba dang // dmyal bar nges par bsreg 'gyur zhes// mkha' 'gro kun dang mnyam sbyor ba'i// rdo rje mkha 'gro bde ba'i mchog/
6'a3(rgyud): rdo rje sems dpa' de bzhin gshegs// bcom ldan rdo rje can gyis gsungs// rgyud kyi rgyal po chen po dpal rdo rje mkha' 'gro lA// de kho na nyid snang ba dam pa'i yul la
6'a4(rgyud): 'jug pa'i ye shes zhes bya ba ste// rim pa phye ba dang po'o// // de nas bcom ldan 'das la/ btsun mo rnams kyis slar yang mchod cing phyag byas
6'a5(rgyud): nas// 'di skad ces gsol to// bcom ldan 'das snying po gang gis/ de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bstan pa 'bral ba'i lha la sogs pa'i gdag pa can rnams dang /
6'a6(rgyud): skye bo gdug pa can gzhan dag dang / 'joms pa dang / zhum par byed pa dang / ltung bar zhi bar bya te/ byang chub kyi snying po'i bar du gnod pa byed par mi 'gyur ba'isnying po
6'a7(rgyud): sdang ba thams cad rab tu 'joms pa lha'i bshad du gsol// de nas bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje'i bdag pos glu
6'a8(rgyud): blangs te 'di skad gsung so// dang po rnam par snang mdzad gnas// der ni sde tshan rnams kyi mtha'// ta dang ba'i ya d+ha b+ha'i mtha'// dbyangs kyi gsuM bas spyir brgyan pa'i// sa
6'b1(rgyud): yi mtha' ni rang gis lta/ la sa'i dbus kyi stan zhugs pa'i// sa yi mtha' ni sbyar bar bya// mda' gnyis kyis ni rnam par sbyang // a stan gnas pa sa yi mtha'// slar yangs
6'b2(rgyud): mtha' mnga' bstan// zla ba'i dum bu thig les brgyan// la sa'i dbus gnas sa bon ni// mnga' bcu yis ni yongasu sbyangs// sa dang sa'i dbus gnas la// zhal gsuM
6'b3(rgyud): gyis ni brgyan pa dang // rlung gi phyogs gnas sa bon la/ ru tra yis ni rnam par brgyan// hUM hUM ha ni bzung nas su// dbyangs kyi dgu pas yang dag dag/ phaT ces
6'b4(rgyud): bya ba dgod par bya/ lhag ma ha yi rkang pa la// lnga ma'i dbus gnas de nyid te// de la ha dza zhes bya'o// ra stan la gnas pa yi mtha'// i zhes bya ba'i mda' dang
6'b5(rgyud): sbyar// slar yang ba zhes bya ba'i mtha'// mda' ni slar bas yongasu sbyang // sa mtha' der ni re zhig zhon// e zhes bya ba rna ba'i brgyan// i dbyangs zla dum thig
6'b6(rgyud): las brgyan// yi ge ra zhon pa yi mtha'// slar yang mtha' sgra lngar ldan/ zla du thig les cod pan brgyan// slar yang de nyid mgon po bzla// rin tshon mtha' ma phaT
6'b7(rgyud): kyis brgyan// rnam par rnang mdzad sna tshogs kyis// tshig rnams kun la dgang bya zhes/ dpa' bo rtag dang mnyam sbyor ba'i// mkha' 'gro ma yi dra ba'i sdom// rdo rje
6'b8(rgyud): sems dpa' de bzhin gshegs// bcom ldan rdo rje can gyis gsungs// dpa' bo rtug dang mnyam sbyor ba'i// mkha' 'gro ma yi dra ba'i sdom// sna tshogs pad ma'i
7a1(rgyud): @nyi dkyil la// der ni hUM las byung ba yi// las kyi rdo rje'i dbus gnas par// hUM gi de nyid rnam bsgom pa'o// 'od zer sna tshogs 'bar ba las/
7a2(rgyud): mkha' 'gro ma'i 'khor spro ba'o// zhal cig phyag gnyis spyan gsum pa// sku mdog dmar po drag chen mo// mdung gi dbyibs can 'jigs pa'i gzugs// spyan dmar
7a3(rgyud): kham skra gyen du mdzes// lang tsho phun sum tshogs par ldan// stag gi spags pa'i nam bza' can// ljags 'dril bas ni cher 'jigs te// 'jigs pa dag kyang
7a4(rgyud): 'jigs par mdzad// mkha' 'gro kun dang mnyam sbyor ba// rdo rje mkha' 'gro rab grags zhes// rdo rje sems dpa' de bzhin gshegs/ bcom ldan rdo rje can gyis gsung
7a5(rgyud): sngon bsags las ni mthar byed pa/ me dang bcas te lan gnyis bzla/ ku ru ku ru sems dpa' bral// ral pa gya gyur ban da gsal// de ni slar yang bzlas
7a6(rgyud): par bya// 'jig rten gzugs dang bral ba yi// tra sa ya zhes bya ste brdzun/ dam pa de ni lan gnyis bzla/ kra sha zhes pa oM sgrar ldan/ glo na b+ha ya yang dag gnas
7a7(rgyud): de yang slar ni bzlas par bya// ma'i mtha' ni nyi stan gnas/ mnga' bcu zla dum thig les dgang // de yang slar ni brjod par bya// 'od byed sbyangs pa yi ni mtha'//
7a8(rgyud): gshegs su gsol ba glo na gnas/ nyis 'gyur du ni bya ba yin// zla zhon thig gsal phe zhes bya// de yang slar ni bzlas par bya// phaT ces bya ba bgyings te bsgrab
7b1(rgyud): rnam par rtog pa kun gyi shing // da ha da ha'i mkha' 'gro'i sdom/ lnga sde'i thog ma gnyis dang ldan/ sde gtso de'i slar bzlas bya/ bkra bak+ka zhes bya dang // ba sa ru
7b2(rgyud): rtswa ti ra an tra/ ma la b+ha la pi ne dang // gr-ih+Na gr-ih+Na sa ba ta ste/ pa ta la g+ha ta pu dza g+haM/ sa paM ba tang tsa ya nyis 'gyur bya// a dang ka'i yi ge dang / gsum pa
7b3(rgyud): yi ni gsum par sbyar/ bzhi pa de ni rlung la gnas// lan gnyis su ni bzlas par bya// sa yi mtha' ni nyi mar gnas/ yi ge bzhi pas dgang bar bya/ slar
7b4(rgyud): yang de ni lan gnyis bzla/ lnga sde mtha' yi stan bzhugs pa// ka sha a dang thig ler ldan// sa bon de ni gnyis bzlas bya/ sa mtha' mda' gnyis dang ldan pa//
7b5(rgyud): slar yang sa mtha' mda' gsum sbyar// de bzhin sa mtha' mda' lnga'i stan/ de kun zla ba'i dum bu dang // thig le yis ni cod pan brgyan// de dag yang yang
7b6(rgyud): basbyar bar bya// ka sa tsa dang de rnams ni/ i sgra yi ni mchog gis gzung // li yi mtha' ni re re sbyar/ de dag kyang ni yang yang basbyar// u sgra la zhon sa yi mtha'/
7b7(rgyud): slar yang zla dum thig les sbyangs// phaT ces bya ba'i rin chen bsgrub/ chang dang min sna tshogs pa'i/ me tog mang po yang dag zin/ de dag lha mo sgyu ma che/ dngos grub
7b8(rgyud): thams cad rab ster ba'o// 'di ni gsungs pa tsam gyis kyang / 'jig rten khams kun g.yos gyur cing // de bzhin gshegs pa kun bsgrag nas/ slar yang de bzhin/
8a1(rgyud): ngo mtho @#gshegs pa kun/ byang chub tu ni mngon sangs rgyas/ ri bo thams cad 'dar zhing gas// ma mo'i tshogs dang 'byung po'i tshogs/
8a2(rgyud): gdon dang rims dang dbyig dug dang / gnod sbyin srin po log 'dren tshogs/ sdang ba thams cad btul zhing bcom// zhi 'gyur bkug ste dkyil 'khor gyi/
8a3(rgyud): dbus su bcug ste dam tshig gis/ bcings nas kyang ni dbang du mdzad/ dmyal ba ya ni sdig pa kun/ dral te nges bcom bsnyil mo zhes/ mkha' 'gro kun dang
8a4(rgyud): mnyam sbyor ba'i// rdo rje mkha' 'gro bde ba'i mchog/ rdo rje sems dpa' de bzhin gshegs/ bcom ldan rdo rje can gyis gsungs// gru bzhi pa la sgo bzhi pa/
8a5(rgyud): sgo skyong dong ni yang dag ldan/ de dbus pad ma bri bya ba/ 'od zer dmar chen gsal ba'i mdangs/ phyi rol ri mo bzlum pos bskor/ de yi dbus su bcom ldan 'das/
8a6(rgyud): khro bo chen po zhal bzhis brgyan/ zhal gyi mche ba bcung zad brtsigs// khro dang bcas shing bshad pa'i zhal/ g.yas pa dkar zhing zhi ba ste// g.yon pa dmar po
8a7(rgyud): cher 'jigs pa// rgyab ni 'od zer ser po'i mdog/ phyag bzhi yis ni brgyan pa ste/ dpa' bo g.yon na kha T+wAM dang // de bzhin du ni thong pa snams// g.yas na 'bar ba'i rdo rje dang /
8a8(rgyud): khyab par du ni shor gyis brgyan// rig ma bzhi dang yang dag ldan/ sangs rgyas gzugs kyis nye bar brgyan// dpa' bo'i shes rab dga' mdzes ma// mda' dang zhug ni bsnams
8b1(rgyud): pa ste// sems dpa' sngon po 'bar ba'i dngos// 'od kyi dkyil 'khor dmar po can/ dung khrod me ltar gsad mthong zhing // 'jigs pa yi ni dus ltar drag/ me ltar 'bar ba'i

14b8(rgyud): ha ra ha ra na ga naM/ pra ha ra pra ha ra/ sarba na ga naM/ tshin d+ha tshin d+ha na ga naM/ hr-i da ya ni/ b+hin d+ha b+hin d+ha na ga mar mi/ bi shir yan du ga hri da yi ni spo nga ya s+pho da ya ga na ya/ na ni bi shi
15a1(rgyud): yan te na ga sha ri ra ni ka tad ya tha/ hUM hUM phaT na ga si d+ha ra na ya phaT/ da ka ud s+ya d+ha na ya phaT ni lam ba sa na ya phaT/ a pra ti ha tA ba la ba
15a2(rgyud): kr-i ma pa phaT/ kr-i tan ta ru pa pha phaT/ ro sha sha ya saT/ tra sa na pha baT/ ku swa ngo tshad na ka ra ya phaT/ pre ta pi sha tsa bi na sa na ka ra ya phaT/ yak+Sha a pa sma ra bi na sa na ka ra ya
15a3(rgyud): paT/ ha sa ha sa da ra da ra ma ra ya/ na sa ya na sa ya/ sarba bi ga na bi na ya ka na phaT/ ni la da ra ba ro badz+ra pA ne/ ad dz+nyA pa ya ti swahA/ gnod sbyin dang / srin po la sogs
15a4(rgyud): pas zin pa la ne/ chu la bzlas te gtor na grol bar 'gyur ro// char zlog pa la ni/ tha la ba la ni bzlas nas sprin la bltas te gtor bar bya'o// chu la bzlas te gtor na ni char 'ab
15a5(rgyud): par 'gyuraro// rims la ni skud pa sngon po la bzlas te gtor na grol bar 'gyur ro// zla ba dang nyi ma gzas zin pa'i dus su/ go ro can la lan stong mngon par bzlas te/ dpral bar
15a6(rgyud): thig le byas nas srung bar 'gyuro// don la dmigs te gcang ni nga gtsang ma'i gos gyon la/ nyin mtshan du kun tu ru bsreg te/ lan brgyad brgya bzlas na/ rmi lam du dge sdig thams
15a7(rgyud): cad ston par 'gyuraro// sa la lan bdun bzlas te chom po la bltas nas bus na/ chom po bas mi mthong zhing bzlog par 'gyur ro// me tog gi 'bras bu la lan bdun bzlas te gang la
15a8(rgyud): byin pa de dbang du gyu ro zhes// mkha' 'gro kun dang mnyam sbyor ba'i// rdo rje mkha' 'gro bde ba'i mchog/ rdo rje sems dpa' de bzhin gshegs// bcom ldan rdo rje can gyis gsung //
15b1(rgyud): rgyud kyi rgyal po chen po dpal rdo rje mkha' 'grolas// klu bams cad dgug pa'i ris par bye ba ste// gsum pa'o// de nas bcom ldan 'das la lha mo rnams kyis mtshad
15b2(rgyud): cing phyag byas te/ 'di skad ces gsol to// las thams cad kyi tshogs bcom ldan 'das lha yis gshad du gsol// de nas bcom ldan 'das kyis rig pa'i rgyal po 'di
15b3(rgyud): mgur du bzhes te bka' stsal pa/ gI li gi li ba dza bar sha sa pa ya da ni bar sha ba ya da pa da yi ni bar sha bar sha sa pa ya hUM hUM hUM hAM ho ho ho/ bu sa tha bu sa tha bu sa tha ha saM ha
15b4(rgyud): sa ha sa/ oM ni bzla phyed thig les brgyan// de ri rku 'dzin brgyad la gnas/ mkha' 'gro ma'i rigs sngags te// sgyu ma chen mo'i rang bzhin no// 'di

15b6(rgyud): ma sa na ba si ni ma hA ka la a nu ra tsa ya/ tad ya tha/ oM tsa le tsa la pra tsa le la la la la ya de ba la gaM sa hA// rdo rje sngags 'di bsnyen pa khri byas te// mtshan phyed na ling
15b7(rgyud): ga'i drung du ji srid 'ongs kyi bar du bzlas pa byas te/ gong bu dgug pa'i cho ga'o// oM tsa mun te du ma ke shaM baM dud dzaM b+he ha na \u0f7f mang ha ra ha ba Ta pa cad btang ta a na ya swAd+ya/
15b8(rgyud): rang gi rkang 'thil g.yon pas sen rtsis ri rab bris la/ de'i nang rol gyi grwa bzhir yig hri bzhi bri/ dbus su sngags kyi tshig bris la/ rdog pas mnar te bzlas na// khugs shing dbang du/
16a1(rgyud): 'gyu ro// skyes bu byin pa g.yon pa'i rus pa'i thur ma la/ steng gi char tshogs kyi dbang phyug phyag bzhi pa/ zhal 'og tu gzigs pa/ lag pa g.yas pa dang g.yon/
16a2(rgyud): par tho ba dang dgra ta dang zhags pa dang gdung rtse gsum pa bsnams pa byas la/ dug dang khrag dang skyes che dang lan tsA dang / ce myang tshar bcas pa'i mar nag gi nang da/ phur bu de
16a3(rgyud): gtses te/ stobs po che'i sngags bzlas la/ gang gi khyim sgor sbas pa de gcong nad chen po dang 'byung ba gnas par 'gyur la/ gton na thar par 'gyuraro// oM badz+ra kro Ta ma hA pa la ha
16a4(rgyud): na da ha pa tsa bi da sa ya/ u da ya ma ya hUM phaT// / grog 'khar gyi sa dang / ba'i rnams bcas pas/ kU ba su kA'i gzugs bstan mtho gang tsam la byas te/ ka ra bi ri'i lcug mas bka'
16a5(rgyud): la/ gu gul gyi gdug pa rgyun mi 'chad par 'dug cing / dkar gsum gyi gtor ma sbyin la/ ka ra bi ra'i lhag mas rgyun mi chad par chu gtor zhing bzlas na/ zhag bdun gyis char gyi
16a6(rgyud): rgyun 'beb par byed do// ji ste bab par ma gyur na nyi ma bdun pa la dub bu dum bu byas te/ bum pa'i nang du blug la/ ts+tsha bzhi pa'i sngags de la bzlos shing chu bo chen po'i bskur na/
16a7(rgyud): nges par 'bab par 'gyur ro// oM ga ga a ri ga ga swA hA// sngags 'das nang bar gdong ma bkrus par rde'u la lan bdun bzlas te gar yang rung ba'i bu gar bcug la/ che ge me'i kha ching
16a8(rgyud): shig ces brjod na/ kha cings par 'gyu ro// mu kha ti than ti mu ka tshan ti/ mu ka ka dan ti/ laM laM ka mu ka naM/ mu tra pu ri she na de ba ta sa mu khaM ban da ni swA hA// glang gi gtsi ba sa la ma lhang
16b1(rgyud): ba byi ba'i khung bu sgo gnam du bltas pa'i nang du bcug la/ bzlas shing kha chings shig ces brjod na/ rgyal po'i phro brang la sogs pa dang / shags 'gyed pa la bzlas pa tsam gyis kha
16b2(rgyud): btsang bar 'gyur ro// a kha ro mu khaM thog mar sbur/ sarba d+harma naM de mthar// rab ta sbar te slar yang ni// a mud pan nad tad ces bya/ sngon du gsung pa'i sbyor ba ya / blo gros chen mo
16b3(rgyud): mdun nunas te/ sngags 'di bdun ni brjod byas na/ mkhar gnas rnams kyis nges par nani/ chu ni rab tu mang po 'bebs// sde mtshan gyi mtha' ma ra'i stan la gnas pa la/ dbyangs yig
16b4(rgyud): bzhi pa dang / thig les brgyan te/ tsan dan dmar pos nyal ba'i sngas kyis bzhi la byugs te/ der rang gi khrag gis snying po la ming bris la nyal ba'i dus su me tog dmar po gtor zhing bdug pa
16b5(rgyud): bdug na/ rang gi bud med chags pA mi byed par gyu ro// snying gar nyi ma la hUM bsgoms te// bdag nyid kham gsuM rnam par rgyal ba la sogs par bsgos la/ rdo rje so can gyi khrag gis shing dza ti'i lcug
16b6(rgyud): ma'i myu gus/ ras sam gro ga la sa bon gyi dbus su// bsgrub bya'i ming dang bskal tshig du bcas pa hAM ta gi zhes bya ba'i sa bon gnyis kyi dbusu bris la// lhag kyu la sog pas dgug pa la sog pa'i les byas
16b7(rgyud): te/ so phag gi dbus bcug la skud pa dmar rdo bkris nas/ rlung 'tsham su g.yon rgyang gi nang pas mnan te bzlas na/ rgya mtsho la thug gis bzhi thams cad du 'khyams par 'gyu ro// gton nas 'o
16b8(rgyud): mas bkrus na grol bar 'gyur gyi/ gzhan du ni ma yin no// bdag nyid mi dmar po las bud med kyi gzugs bskyed de/ oM dmar po spyi bor yang bsams la/
17a1(rgyud): bu mo'i kha nas bdag nyid kyi khar sngags kyi phreng ba cho ga bzhin du bzhags par bsam na/ dbang du 'gyur ro// bud med kyi bcing ba'i shul gyis dang / rang
17a2(rgyud): gi gci ba'i shal gyi sa las mo mtshan gyi gzugs byas te/ de'i steng du rang gi mtshan ma bzhag la/ sngags lan bdun bzlas nas/ der gci ba'i las byas la/ nyi ma bdun du dus gsum du sngags
17a3(rgyud): brgya rtsa brgyad bzlas na/ brgya byin gyi chung ma yang 'ong bar 'gyur na/ gzhan rnams lta ci smos/ skyes pa'i thod par go ro tsa na dang sen rtsis bsgrub bya'i gzugs brnyan bris te/ snying khar ming dang spel ba'i sngags
17a4(rgyud): bris la/ dri'i chus byugs nas/ thod pa gnyis kha sbyar cing ro'i skud pas kun tu dkris te/ sgra tshil gyis byugs la/ ro bsregs pa'i sol ba'i me la/ ji srid spa tshil zhu bar ma gyur gyi bar du/ rig pa'i rgyal po 'di
17a5(rgyud): bzlos shing gdungs na/ las kyi cho ga de ltar yang / lha'i 'jig rten yang 'ong bar 'gyur ro// dug can gyi thod par gnod sbyin ston pa'i lce bcug la/ rta'i mig pa'i ser khar gtsug nas/ gang
17a6(rgyud): gi khyim sgor sbas pa de nyi ma bdun gyis bskrad par 'gyur ro// yang na las kyi dus su kha zas kyi phud kyi chang bu la/ sngags lan brgya rtsa brgyad bzlas te khro ba dang bcas pas bsgrub bya gzhug
17a7(rgyud): ste/ zhi ma bdun gyis bskrad par 'gyur ro// rtsi ba sa las ma lhung ba las bsgrub bya'i gzugs brnyan sor bcu drug pa'am/ phyed dang bcu gsum pa byas la/ ras ma'i dum bu la de'i ming bris
17b1(rgyud): te ltor bcug la/ bag zan gyis de'i kha bkab ste/ re'i bskus bkris la gtun shing la sngags lan bdun bzlas te/ khro ba dang bcas pas de'i gdong btsogs na/ bcing bar 'gyur ro// dbo g.yul du
17b2(rgyud): bsad pa'i ras la bu mo'i gzugs brnyan bris te/ ba glang gi rdul dang shing bu pa ta la'i rtsa ba'i bdug pas bdug na bu mo de 'ong bar 'gyuraro// ras saM gro ga'am spang leb bam rtsig ngos la/ khro bo gshin rje bshed
17b3(rgyud): kyi gzugs kha dog thams cad dang ldan pa/ g.yas brkyang bas mnan pa/ lag pa g.yas na tho ba/ g.yon sbrul zhags 'dzin pa khro gnyer dang smin ma bcum pa/ mche ba rtsigs shing spyan dmar ba/ skra gyen du 'gre
17b4(rgyud): zhing sbrul gyi rgyan gyis brgyan pa/ 'od 'bar ba dang bcas pa bris la/ sbrul zhags kyi ltor dud khrod kyi sol bas dgra'i tshogs kyi ming sngags dang spel ba bris te/ bzhag na ji srid gnas kyi bar du dgra rnam
17b5(rgyud): bcings par 'gyur te/ tha na yid kyi kyang ba cung zad tsam yang gnod par sems par mi 'gyur ba'i/ gal te gnod par sems na/ 'byung po dang rims dang gdon dang sha za dang mkha'agro mas nye bar mche bar
17b6(rgyud): 'gyur la/ lha rnams kyis kyang gtong bar 'gyur te/ pha rol gyi dpung gi tshig dang spel na/ dpung bcing bar 'gyur ro// gzhan yang shing la sogs pa la/ sngags phreng gnyis su bris te/ phreng gnyis pa'i

18a1(rgyud): @#/ du sras nas/ sas thug pa kho nar bkab na/ dgra bcings par 'gyur ba las gzhan du ma yin no// rad na badz+ra zhes byas nas/ de nas oM dang badz+ra brjod hri dang phaT ni mthar

18a6(rgyud): mo bya rog tshang du 'gro kha ma la zar gtsug na/ nges par bskrad par 'gyur ro// rtsig ngos sam spang leb la yi ge pha bri/ de'i nang du dbyangs kyi yi ge 'khor bar bri/ de'i nang du pa bri/ de'i nang du ka bri/ de'i nang du ka thi/
18a7(rgyud): de yi nang du bsgrub bya'i ming bris la/ de kha bcad te bzhag na/ dbang du 'gyur zhing bcing bas bcings par 'gyur ro// lto ba'i pad+ma'i dbus su/ ming gi yi ge 'am/ a bsgoms te pad+ma'i bsdu ba byas la/

20b2(rgyud): pad mar ga lta bur yi/ g.yon zhal 'od zer tshogs kyis ni// thams cad ma lus bsreg snam sems// ban du ka'i me tog gi/ phungs po spungs 'dri'i 'od kyis ni// rigs gsum las
20b3(rgyud): byung kun nas ni/ lhags pa thams cad ngo mtshar gyur// 'od gzugs de ni bsreg snyam sems// nyi ma stong pas lhag 'od kyis// bskal zhing byang chub thob par mdzad// phaT sgra chen

22a1(rgyud): 'gro ma'i 'khor lo dang // rdo rje gsum gyi rang bzhan rnams// spro bas ma mkha' gsal mdzad pa// phyag brgyad sran gsum gyen ska 'bar// mkha'
22a2(rgyud): 'gro nyi shu bzhi phyed bskor// de ltar sngags pas rnam pa sam bya// g.yas dang po ni rdo rje sngon po 'bar zhing rno ba gdengs pa la// rigs ldan gyis bkris pa bsnams pa'o// gnyis pa
22a3(rgyud): na pad mas bcings pa'i mda'i mchog go// gsum pa na pad+ma chen pos yu ba bkris pa'i la gri'o// bzhi pa na dung skyong gi zhags pas dkris pa'i lugs kyu'o// g.yon gyi dang po na mtha'
22a4(rgyud): yas kyi ba dan btags pa'i kha T+wAM bsgreng ba'o// gnyis pa na nor rgyas kyi bu l+li rgyud byas pa'i gzhu'i mchog go/ gsum pa na 'jog po zhags pa dang sdig 'dzub po// bzhi pa na tshangs pa'i
22a5(rgyud): mgo bo khrag 'dzag pa stobs kyi rgyus bcings pa bsnams pa'o// klu'i rgyal po de thams cad kyang mche ba gtsigs shing lce 'dril ba// blta ba'i dug can/ gdengs ka'i nor bu'i 'od kyi nam
22a6(rgyud): mkha'i ngos thams cad gsal ba'o// khwa gdong ma las sogs pa thams cad kyang sbrul gyis brgyan cing klubs shing spun gsum pa skra gyen du 'bar ba// phyag na zangs gri dang thod pa
22a7(rgyud): ba bsnams pa/ zod pa'i phreng bas klubs shing / gcer bu kal ba gzigs pa/ 'od zer sna tshogs 'phro ba/ khro gnyir gyi rim pa can/ zur mig du gzigs pas sa bani bskyod pa
22a8(rgyud): klu'i tshogs skrag pas kha bub du 'gyel bar bas mA pas nam mkha' la gnas te char gyi rgyun gtong bas sa bzhi skad cig gis gang bar byedo zhes/ mkha' 'gro kun dang mnyam sbyor ba'i
22b1(rgyud): mkha' 'gro ma ni 'bar ba'i mchog/ rdo rje sems dpa' de bzhin gshegs/ bcom ldan rdo rje can gyi gsungs// yang na rta bla mo zhib du btags la/ ras kyi g.yogs te li
22b2(rgyud): khri dang sres la sbrang rtsis sbrus te mgo bdun pa'i klu'i gzugs sor bcu gnyis pa byas la// de'i khang pa sor bcu drug yangs par byas nas khang pa de bul+lIl gdong bzhi byas te/ grwa gcing
22b3(rgyud): pa la ni rta'i gdong pa gnyis pa la sngo ge'i gdong ba/ gsum pa la spre'u yi gdong pa/ bzhi pa la nya'i gdod pa byas ste/ de'i nang du'i' klu'i rgyal po ras kha dog sna tshogs pas g.yog
22b4(rgyud): te bzhag la/ de nas snga ga brgya rtsa brgyad yongs su bzlas pas btab te/ yid kyis ji gas ltar 'dod pa'i me tog dang bdug pa drang gtor ma las sogs pa'i mchod pa bsam te byin la/
22b5(rgyud): yungs kar la lan bdun sngags te klu'i steng na gtor te/ de nas 'dod pa thams cad pa'i gtor ma byin na/ des klu'i rgyal po rnams mdza' bor gyur nas/ klu thams cad kyis than pa byung
22b6(rgyud): ba'i dus su nyi ma bdun du char phab pas/ 'dzam bu'i gling thams cad gang bar byed de/ char mi 'bab pa'i dus su de ltar byas na/ gdon me za bar char dab po/ ji ste klu gdug pa can
22b7(rgyud): yin na yang / rlung grang me dang rje char dang klog dang ser ba 'bebs te de bzlog par 'dod na/ rig pa 'dzin pa'i yungs kar dang thal ba zho gnyis tsam la/ lan nyi shu'i bar du bzlas te/
22b8(rgyud): ji srid 'dod pa'i sa phyogs su 'tshams bcings la/ yang de nyid la na 'dun bzlas te klu'i mgor bsnun zhing / yid kyis ji snyed 'dod par phyags bcing bar bya ste/ phyogs 'tsham
23a1(rgyud): zhodang steng 'og gtor na/ mtshams chen po bcing bar 'gyur ro// ji ste dgra thams cad dang 'gran dang zla dang sdang ba'i grogs po dang / sdang ba'i phyogs byed/
23a2(rgyud): pa rnams dang / pha rol gyi 'khor lo 'jigs shing gdul bar 'dod pa dang / btags pa dang / bcing ba dang / gsad pa dang / reng pa dang / gzhom par 'dod na/ rta bla
23a3(rgyud): mo de nyid dung khrod kyi thal ba dang bsgos te/ skyes pa 'am bud med kyi gzugs byas la/ khro bo chen po'i sngags brgya rtsa brgyad zlas te/ dur khrod kyis brkos pa'i nang du ming nas
23a4(rgyud): smos te bzhag la/ yungs kar la brgya rtsa brgyad bzlas te de'i steng du gtor nas seng ldeng gi phur ba la lan brgya rtsa brgyad bzlas te btab nas sbas na/ ji srid phur bu ma gton gyi
23a5(rgyud): bar du sdug bsngal chen po nyamasu myong bar 'gyur te/ rig pa 'dzin pa ma btogs pa/ gzhan gyis grol bar mi nus so/ ji ste gsad par 'dod na mi rus kyi phur bu pa
23a6(rgyud): sngags brgya rtsa brgyad bzlas pas snun la/ khrag dang bcas pa'i yungs kar la zlas te gtor na/ zhag bdun sdod par mi 'gyur ro zhes/ mkha' 'gro kun dang mnyam bskor ba'i//
23a7(rgyud): rdo rje mkha' gro bde ba'i mchog/ rdo rje sems dpa' de bzhin gshegs/ bcom ldan rdo rje can gyis gsungs/ rgyud kyi rgyal po chen po dpal rdo rje mkha'agro bas// klu thams cad dgug
23a8(rgyud): pa dang bzhug pa dang bcing ba'i cho ga rgyas pa ste/ rim par phye ba lnga pa'o// // de nas bcom ldan 'das la lha mo rnams kyis slar yang mchod cing phyag byas te/ 'di skad ces
23b1(rgyud): gsol to// sgra chen pos rnam par 'phrul pa'i klu'i sngags mi 'chal na/ dka' drin chen pos ga sha du gsol/ bka' stsal pa/ sngags kyi rgyal po chen po'i mtshan nyid skal pa/
23b2(rgyud): chen mo'i lha mo nyon cig/ gshin rje mche ba can ma nyid// rus sbal gyis ni bstan la bzhugs// uSh+ma yi ni tha ma nyid// slar yang bzhi pa la gnas pa// gshin rje'i phyogs kyi
23b3(rgyud): mthar gnas pa ka/ bzang po yis ni steng du brgyun// slar yang gshin rje'i mche ba can/ rus sbal gyis ni rab tu brgyan// oM b+ha zhes bya ba'i tshig dang ldan/ dang po dang ni rub sbal
23b4(rgyud): gyis// stan bzhugs mgon po ri mo dang // rtse sa brgyan lan gnyis bsgyur bar bya// mgon po phan tshun tshigs gis 'bar// ka khi mu khi/ mu ka ke mai nag mgi/ i d+hu b+hag gi/ kot+ti/ sa
23b5(rgyud): be hi ba Di hi/ a pa ri'o si'o// ka ha ka he dzI/ ka smad thaM dza'i ya in da b+ha ma bdi thu ma he sa ro/ pa tsa gle be/ sa ba la ba ha Ne bi ho bi Na sa na ta ha Na se'i/ ka ki hi ya ya pa ri san thi ya zhes/
23b6(rgyud): mkha' 'gro kun dang mnyam sbyor ba'i/ rdo rje mkha' gro bde ba'i mchog/ rdo rje sems dpa' de bzhin gshegs// bcom ldan rdo rje can gyis gsungs// 'bugs byed la ni sa dbang phyug/
23b7(rgyud): zla ba'i dum bus brgyan pa ste/ slar yang dbu' mi'i dbu'i ma bzung // byang phyogs kyi ni dbu ma yi/ zhabs kyi pad+ma nyi ma ldan/ bden bral ba ni sme bas brgyan// 'bar ba 'bugs pas
23b8(rgyud): rnam par klubs/ byang phyogs kyi ni dang po dang / khyu mchog steng na gnas pa yi/ gshin rje phyogs kyi mthar gnas dang // rung ni yu sa mo'i brgyan/ bden bral la ni gnas pa yi//
24a1(rgyud): @#gshin rje'i ni mche ba can/ gti mug brgyan gyi rnam par brgyan// gshin rje 'joms ma gti mug klubs// klu'i phyag rgya 'di yis ni/ mkha'agro ma kun dga'
24a2(rgyud): 'gur 'gyur// sgyu 'phrul chen po bcu drug 'di// yi ge re re kun gnas zhes/ mkha'agro ma kun mnyam sbyor ba'i/ rdo rje sems dpa' de bzhin gshegs// bcom ldan rdo rje can gyis
24a3(rgyud): gsungs/ dang po rus sbal gzung bar bya// bzang po'i steng du gnas pa yi// byang gi dang po gnyis par ldan/ gshin rje pho nya chu ltar bzhugs// yi ge ra ni gti mug brgyan//
24a4(rgyud): slar yang ka sha zhes bya brjod/ gshin rje chen can bzang pos brgyan// slar yang mche can bden bral bzhugs// gti mug ni lhan cig ldan/ der ni sa mthar zhes bya ba/ gti mug
24a5(rgyud): gis ni lhan cig brgyan// lha mo bsten pa 'di yis ni/ bu mo rnams ni dgug pa'i mchog/ shar phyogs nas ni brgyad bzung zhing // bzhi par ldan pa'i dbu mi'i mtha'// yugs
24a6(rgyud): sa me'i spyi bos brgyan// slar yang dbu mi'i mtha' ma bzung // 'bugs pa dang ni ldan par bya// gshin rje 'joms ma bzung nas su// yugs sa mo'i rna cha bya// mthar
24a7(rgyud): gyi sA has yongasu brgyan/ rig byed kyis ni mnyes par bya// zong ba'i dbu granas rgyal bar 'gyur/ mu i NI kA ka k+Sha sak+Shi i ka mu ka ni/ ru pa te sa a i ka mu b+hi nI ho ha pa la ha
24a8(rgyud): laM ma ri ka ni le a haM/ mu ba ka De spa i a bi mung taM ka gri s+ya t+ya mu ga hats+tsha/ u ka tha ke pa ya nA tha mi su sa kham ha phaT// klu'i phyag rgya 'di yis ni/ bcing ba dang ni
24b1(rgyud): bskrad par 'gyur/ oM in de na ha da ba ya/ dza me na u pa sa ya dz+re a/ hri d+ha pra ma dan te na/ tad dzI ya su la ha re na su li yA swA hA/ oM dza d+hi ni dza d+he hi/ ai re ba ni thaM b+ha hi/ oM ma/
24b2(rgyud): ha ni mo ha he na/ oM a kar sha ni a kar she hi/ oM tham pa tham pa ma ha tham pa/ oM mu kaM tham pa ya swA hA/ de ltar rnal 'byor pa rnams kyi cho ga bzhin// lnga bstan pa'o// oM na mo d+ha
24b3(rgyud): b+ha ba te tsa mun te sus kha mu khi/ su Sha kan the/ g+han d+ha da ri a mu ka saM/ mu khaM b+han d+ha hA nA ha na da ha da ha pa tsa pe tsa hUM phaT swA hA// / mkha'agro kan dang mnyam sbyor ba'i/ rdo rje mkha'agro bde
24b4(rgyud): ba'i mchog/ rdo rje sems dpa' de bzhin gshegs/ bcom ldan rdo rje can gyis gsungs// dpa' bo 'dod phyogs su bltas pa'i rkang 'thil gyi lpags pa dang / ma na dang / nyan pa dang /
24b5(rgyud): mig sman dang / rdo dang / dmar po rnams/ mi khrag dang / btags la/ slar yang tsan dan dmar po dang len mang du sbal te/ a ma'i ri lur gyur pa dang / dbus su ling bu ming
24b6(rgyud): bcug ste grib ma la skams nas/ nyi ma dang zla ba dang sreg byed kyi dbus su ri lu bcug la/ slar yang skar ma rgyal la lhag par gnas rla bya ste/ rig pa'i rgyal po'i kal du bcug
24b7(rgyud): pa/ ji srid mi snang bar gyur pa de srid du bzlas par bya'o// sbrul gyi rgyal po rnyed pa dang / ri mo dkar nag dum bu sor phyo la/ dkar nag so sor shes par byas pa de dang / shang
24b8(rgyud): ka bus pa dang / a ka ru nag po dang / stong phrag nyi shu rtsa gtsigs ma tshang ba'i sngags bzlas la/ phyis kyang rgya rtsa brgyad bzlas bdug par bya'o// skar ma rgyal gsum la//
25a1(rgyud): snam du byas te/ zla ba yang ngo la dum bu dkar pos bdug go// mar ngo lA ni dum bu nag pos 'dug go// de nas de gyon pa'i lus kyis lan khri bzlas na 'grur/
25a2(rgyud): bar 'gyur te/ dkar po dang nag po'i phyogs la so sor gyon pas mi snang bar 'gyuraro// lha mo de ni dngos grub kyi yon tan gang du 'dod pa der 'gro bar 'gyur zhing gang la 'dod
25a3(rgyud): pa de la 'dod pa sprod par 'gyur ro// de'i kha ni bu gar lig bu mig bcug te/ du ba med par bsregs la/ de tshig pa dang mtshan mo zhib por btags te/ mig la byugs na
25a4(rgyud): khyim gyi me tog mchog ltar gsal la/ rang gi lha'i sngags bzlas na mi mthong bar 'gyuraro// lto 'phye'i rgyal pos bum pa'i khaM bor gyi nang du bcug te ster du sbas la/ de nas
25a5(rgyud): rul zhing zag pa dang ton te/ de'i thod pa'i rus pa bdar te thig ler byas na grib ma yang med par byed do// de zags pa'i sas lus la byugs na/ dug sna tshogs zhi bar byed/
25a6(rgyud): gang gi rdul gyi dri rtag du zhim zhing skra g.ya su 'khyil ba dang / yid du 'ong zhing grib ma bdun dang ldan la/ lus la rma med cing bdun par smra ba dang / yun 'di du mig mi 'dzum
25a7(rgyud): pa de ni lha mo dngos grub byed par 'gyur te/ gzhan yang kha'i dbugs dri zhim zhing rtag tu skyid de bar gnas pa de ni byang chub sems dpa' rnams ltar sbyin pa chen po rtag tu
25a8(rgyud): gtong pas bsgrub pa po rnams sgrub pa'i phyir/ mi ro'i gzugs kyis gnas te/ sems can rnams byin gyis brlabs pa'i phyir/ sangs rgyas shAkya thub pa mya ngan pas
25b1(rgyud): 'angs pa'i gzugs ltar/ phan pas nye bar gnas pa mdun du mngar ba dang yang dag par ldan pa yin no// lha mo de ni dngos grub kyi yon tan thams cad kyi 'byung gnas//
25b2(rgyud): su gyur pas// lce sdud dang / bya rog dang / bya las sogs pa sha zan thams cad kyis kyang bskor te gnas/ yang dbang po'i tshul gyi gzugs de la/ gnod sbyin/
25b3(rgyud): dang srin po dang lha dang yi dgas las sogs pas kun nas bskor te gnas pa/ bsgrub pa po ni shin du mnyam par bzhag pas cho ga de ltar shes par byas
25b4(rgyud): nas/ de'i nying kha na go ro tsa na yod pa blangs te/ rang gi snying po bzlas pas thig le byas na/ steng du dpag tshad bye ba stong phrag gi rab du 'gro zhing slang 'ong la/
25b5(rgyud): rdzu 'phrul dang cho 'phrul sna tshogs mthong zhing / mkha'agro ma rnams dang dga' 'gur rtse zhing rnal 'byor thams cad brnyed par 'gyur ro/ de'i sha zos pa tsam gyis khams
25b6(rgyud): gsum gyi ye shes can du 'gyur zhing / rlung gi shugs kyis dpag tshad rgyar 'gro ba/ lha'i lus can du 'gyur te/ gang gang 'dod pa rang de ster bar 'gyur ro// na mkha'
25b7(rgyud): lding dang byi ba dang 'ug pa'i zhag la/ mi ro'i ras kyi sdong bu byas te/ me mar gtang na/ gter thams cad mdzod par 'gyur zhing / sha dza dang 'byung po gang dag yib
25b8(rgyud): pa de dag thams cad mthong bar 'gyur ro// mkha' gro kun dang mnyam sbyor ba'i// rdo rje mkha' 'gro 'de ba'i mchog/ rdo rje sems dpa' de bzhin gshegs/
26a1(rgyud): bcom ldan rdo rje can gyis gsungs// rgyud kyi rgyal po chen po dpal rdo rje mkha' 'gro mas// klu'i sngags tha mad kyi rab tu sbyor ba'i rim par phye/
26a2(rgyud): ba ste/ drag pa'o// / lag pa'i phyag rgya'i mtshan nyid ni/ de la dus chos bsten par bya// gang zhig/ de nas yang dag bshad byang / gang zhig sti rtsug phre reg/
26a3(rgyud): pa/ de la mgo bo bstan par bya/ gang zhig dpral ba ston byed pa/ de la khus chos bstan par bya/ gang zhig mchu la reg byed pa// de kos ko bstan par bya// de la lteng
26a4(rgyud): bstan par bya/ gang zhig rgung chos ston byed pa/ de la sa ni bstan par par bya/ gang zhig skye gnas ston byed pa// de la ling ga bstan par bya/ gang zhig pus mo ston pa//

26a6(rgyud): gang shig nam mkha' ston byed pa/ de la nyi ma bstan par bya/ gang zhig chu bo ston byed pa/ de la rgya mtsho bstan par bya/ gang zhig rkang pa ston byed pa/ de la 'thil ni bstan par
26a7(rgyud): bya gang zhig sor mo ston byed pa/ de la sen mo bstan par bya/ gang zhig nam mkha' ston byed pa/ de la nyi ma bstan par bya/ gang zhig chu bo ston byed pa/ de la rgya mtsho
26a8(rgyud): bstan par bya/ de gang zhig sor mo cig ston pa/ de la'ang sor mo gnyis bstan bya/ de nas shi ba bso ba dang // gson po nang med spel bya zhing // 'phrog byed ma la sogs
26b1(rgyud): pa yi/ zin pa dang ni grol ba'i rnga// mdor sdus nas na bshang bya yis// de ni lha mo mnyan par gyis/ gang zhig steng du lta byed pa/ de la dpral ba bstan par bya//
26b2(rgyud): gang zhig mig ni ston byed pa/ de la so ni bstan par bya/ gang zhig lte ba ston byed pa// de la mchu ni bston par bya// gang zhig mchu ni ston byed pa// de la che ba bstan par bya
26b3(rgyud): gang zhig lce ni ston byed pa// de la lto ba bstan par bya/ gang zhig byin par ston byed pa// de la rA ni bstan par bya// gang zhig brla ni bston byed pa// de la rkang pa

26b5(rgyud): bya/ gang zhig mdud ni ston byed pa/ de la shag+na snyan par bya/ gang zhig rtse mo ston byed pa/ gang zhig phyogs ni ston byed pa/ de la phyogs 'tshams bstan par bya//

26b8(rgyud): 'gro mar ni nyer 'gro ba'i// 'tshan nyid 'di dag shes par bya// song ba'i sa la sngar mi ldog/ rgyu slar ni du ba dang // de bzhin don med par ni nong // 'dzam par smra zhing
26b9(rgyud): de la lta ba ldan par bya
27a1(rgyud): snying rje med// don med par ni mang du smra// sgyu ma mche dang mnyam sbyor ba'i/ mkha'agro ma ni 'bar ba'i mchog/ mtshan nyid 'di dag dang ldan pa//

27a4(rgyud): zhig lag g.yon ston byed pa// phyag ni 'chal bar byed pa yin// gang zhig srin lag ston byed pa// phyag 'tshal ba'i lan gyur yin// gang zhig lto ba la rdebs pa//

27a7(rgyud): ni bcings par ston pa yin// gang zhig nam mkha' lding la reg pa// bdag ni grol bar ston pa yin// gang zhig lag pas lag pa ston/ de ring gtor ma bza' zhes ston/
27a8(rgyud): gang zhig lag g.yas ston byed pa// de ltar gyis zhes ston pa yin// gang zhig rna ba la rdebs pa// gnas par bya zhes ston pa yin/ de nas dag brda'i cho ga bshad//
27b1(rgyud): po ti gis ni phyag 'tshal ba'o// pra ti po ta gi ni phyag gi lan no// ga mum mi 'gro ba'o// lum pa la ni skyes pa'o// ni ga ram mi byin cig pa'o// tsa bu ka ni long shig pa'o// hrid/
27b2(rgyud): ya ni dpa'o// kur ba ni shi ba'o// kar ni kar ni dril du'o// a li ka ra ni mgo de'o// ba ra hi ni skra'o// shra ba no ni rna ba'o// man tha ni bdud rtsi'o// na ra ni mnyam par
27b3(rgyud): 'gra'o// ta li ka ni mkha' gro ma'o// na ra kaM ni dkyil 'khor ro// a bu kaM ni dur khrod do// ka la khi la ni sgo'o// sA sa ni bram ze'o// pa ri ti ni rgyal rigs so// bi ra di ni rje'u
27b4(rgyud): rig so// TI kU re ni rmang rag so// an tha ni shan pa'o// a pA ka li ni phyug so// da ki ni srin mo'o// mu ta ka ni kUm me'o// lce so la reg pa ni bkres par ston pa'o// tre
27b5(rgyud): sna ni dris bsgo pa'o// a kaM ma nam ni gang nas zhes pa'o// s+tha nang ni che ge mo nas zhes bya ba'o// ki ra no ni me tog go/ lam po da ra dan de ni rgod pa'o/ bi ga nya ba ti ni tshim
27b6(rgyud): pa'o// d+hu ma pri ya na ni chu 'dzin no// sa nu ni ri bo'o// sa ro de ni chu bo'o// ang gu la ni cha shas so// ba da ni ni sdong po'o// ra tsi ka ni lce'o// a da na ni se'o// paM ka te ni
27b7(rgyud): rgyal mtshan no// tshan me ni phreng ba'o// tsa la ni rlung do// me ga ba ti ni phyugs so// man da la ni mnyam pa'o// sA sa ni lam gyi gzhi mdo'o// phal gu sham ni skye ba'o//
27b8(rgyud): ma hA kAr ni phrugs chen po'o// tsha nir lo/ na ni skyes bu'o// ba ni klang ngo // ma ni ma he'o// ba ni bza' ba'o// a s+ya ka ni rgyal po'i skyes bu'o// sgra ni gnas pa'o// kha la/
27b9(rgyud): ro de ni char 'bab pa'o/
28a1(rgyud): reg pa ni zos pa'o// so la reg pa ni ngoms pa'o// tre ka ni ngo tsha ba'o// stong pa la reg pa ni me thun gyis shig pa'o// baR+Sha la reg pa ni de ltar gyis/
28a2(rgyud): shig pa'o// zhes mkha' 'gro kun dang mnyam skor ba'i// rdo rje mkha' 'gro bde ba'i mchog/ rdo rje sems dpa' de bzhin gshegs// bcom ldan rdo rje can gyis gsungs// rgyud

34a5(rgyud): dam// yang na 'byung po'i mtshan mo la// thod pa'i stan la gnas nas su// lho phyogs su ni kha ltas nas// dug dang khrag dang gtum pa yi// sa bon gyis ni snag cha dang //
34a6(rgyud): bar snang la ni thod pa blugs// mi yi rus pa'i smyug gu yis// 'jigs byed 'jigs pa'i sngags rnams btu// dang po sha chen gtor ma sbyin// de nas las ni rtsam
34a7(rgyud): bar bya// dmar po 'am ni sngon po yi// gos ni khyad par dag tu bgo/ mchod pa rdo rje go cha dang // de bzhin bsam gtan zlas pa dag/ ji ltar sus kyang mi rtogs pa/

34b1(rgyud): par bya// stong la stong pa'i pad ma ste// nges par 'joms pa'i grwa ru ni// sngags phreng de bzhin phreng ba yi// rim pa de ltar brjod pa yin// 'di ni khabs gsum rgya/

34b3(rgyud): ni/ bzhin mdzes ma ni khyod la bshad// 'di ni sdang ba thas cad kyi// de bzhin 'jigs byed mi bzad yin// yang dag cho ga gang gis ni// dngos grub myur du
34b4(rgyud): 'jigs byed pa// bza' dang ston mo 'dus pa yi// bsgrub thabs cho ga de nas bshad// phyugs rnams dag ni dgug pa nyid// sgrub pos sngar stan rim pas bya//
34b5(rgyud): rgyu med pa'i phyugs rnams ni// rgyu mtshan med pas bzhom par bya// phyugs rnams dang ni de bzhin lnga// bong bu mi dang rus sbal dang // rnga mo lce sbyang rta la sogs// khyi
34b6(rgyud): dang phag gi sha dag dang / bzangs kyi gtsug phud can de bzhin// bza' dang sbyin bsreg gtor ma ni// ma dpyad par ni byas gyur na// ma lus la med 'grub cing /
34b7(rgyud): rgyal srid thams cad rab 'grub zhes// mkha' 'gro kun dang mnyam sbyor ba'i// rdo rje mkha' 'gro bde ba'i mchog/ rdo rje sems dpa' de bzhin gshegs/
34b8(rgyud): bcom ldan rdo rje can gyis gsungs// rgyud kyi rgyal po chen po dpal rdo rje mkha'agro las// 'khrul 'khor thams cad 'byung ba zhes bya ba'i rim pa phye ba ste//
35a1(rgyud): dbu pa'o// / che dang nad med spel ba dang // bya dang bya min sbyor ba'i mchog/ dbugs kyi las la sogs mtshan nyid// nyon cig/

37a1(rgyud): dbang phyug gi nyi ma la 'chi bar 'gyur ro// sa'i dbang phyug gi nyi ma la btsas pa'i byis pa ni// nyi ma brgyad pa la'o// lo brgyad pa la gal te shi

37a5(rgyud): bsnyon rmongs par byed pa dang / dpa' zhing brtul phod pas pha rol gnon pa dang / dgra thams cad 'joms shing skye bo dam pa dang mdza' ba dang / skyabs med pa rnams kyi dpung

37b1(rgyud): 'khor mang ba dang / yo byad 'phel zhing sdug bsngal mang ba dang / gnyen bdun thams cad dga' ba/ ngan song la rtse ba dang / nor dang / phyugs mang ba/ chung ma gsum len cing /

40a1(rgyud): / mtshan ma ni// rim gyis rim gyis sbyar bar bya// nyin mo'i yi ni chu tshod dag/ mkhas pas bzhi dang bcu gnyis bsgyur// mtshan mo drug dang bcu gsum
40a2(rgyud): dgyur// nu tshod mkhas pas brtsam par bya// re'u mig dag ni gnyis pa la// dus la mkhas pas mtshan ma bya// nyin me drug dang bcu gnyis bsgyur// chu chod
40a3(rgyud): ni mtshan ma bya/ bzhi dang bcu bsum bsgyur ba ni// mtshan me'i chu tshod nyid du rtag/ brgyad dang bcu gnyis sgyur ba dag/ nyin mo ru ni rtag par bya// gnyis dang

40a5(rgyud): mo'-i'i nu tshod shes byas ste// brgyad dang bcu ni gnyis po dag/ de yi mtshan mo'i mtshan mar bya/ bzhi dang bcu gsum mtshan ma ni/ nyin mo yi ni chu rno ste/ drug

53a3(rgyud): mkha' gro mi ni thams cad kyang // the tshom skye na gzhan ci smos// sgyu ma kun tu rnam 'phrul pa/ nyon cig lha mo sgyu ma che// gang zhig bris pa tsam gyis ni// sgrub pos dngos grub
53a4(rgyud): thob gyur pa/ mdor sdus nas ni brjod bya ste// de ni bdag gis bshad gyis nyon// gnag dang dmar rab rtag gyur nas// khyad par du ni gtor ma sbyin// tsa ru'i bza' ba lhan cig/
53a5(rgyud): bya/ 'di yis sgrub po kun la ni// ma mo dga' 'gyur the tshem med// de nas mkha' gro ma rnams ni// sa rnams la ni rnam rol pa// brtson tshon 'khor lo bsgyur ma dang // steng
53a6(rgyud): chen ma deng rab dpa' mo// 'khor le'i go cha blang rnam// kha Da ro ha 'khor lo'i shugs// bya ba dong ma dang rten mo// shin du bzang mo sngo bsangs mo// chang 'thung ma dang rlung
53a7(rgyud): shugs// de bzhin 'jigs byed chen mo dang // sa bsrungs ma dang ljon grib ma// lang ka'i bdag mo mi'u thung mo// 'od ldan ma dang gtum mig mi// rab gtum ma ste bsgrub
53a8(rgyud): byed yin// mkha' gro ma nyi shu bzhi/ 'di dag sngon nyid grub pa yin// rang ming brjod pa'i sngags la ni// mthar ma ni hUM hUM phaT dang sbyar// oM ni thams cad gsal byed de/
53a9(rgyud): dpa' ba'i sgo sa sna chenam
53b1(rgyud): grub gsol 'dod pa thams cad la// rnal 'byor dam chog 'di mthong na// gzhan dag snying po med brtsar mtshungs// dpa' bo nyid gur grub pa ni// dpal ldan he ru ka yi ni/
53b2(rgyud): dkyil 'khor dam pa mthong ba yin/ de nas de shes rtag bsgom pa// dngos grub de bzhin gshegs pas gsungs// nyon cig lha mo she rab can// rig pa'i rgyal mo bsgrub
53b3(rgyud): pa'i thabs// 'khor lo chen po rmad gyur pa// gdeng ka'i dbang phyug zhes bya ste// nges pa tsam gyis bsreg byed na// ming dang ldan par bris pa yis// gding ka thams cad
53b4(rgyud): smos ci dgos// dbang ldan nas ni brtsams nas su// klu rnams sa bon las byung ba// rin chen dang ldan gdengs gsum mtho// gzhan yang phyogs ni kun tu bsam// de mnas
53b5(rgyud): mgur du 'di bzhes te// shar du kra mang bar du dri// nub du de he ste byang du haM// gshin rje hUM zhes pa bri// ki li ki li'i yi dag su// srin dro tsi li si li bri// me yi 'tshangs ni/
53b6(rgyud): mtha' dang bcas// dang po rab tu ma ma nas ni// brtson chen ma'i mthar thug pa// sngags 'di dag ni byin gyis brlag/ 'khor lo 'di ni skal chen ldan// dgra rnams kyi ni
53b7(rgyud): gnang gcod pa// hUM phaT zhes bya spel ba yi// sgrub bya de'i dbu su tri lan cig bzlas pa'i gu gul gyis// bdug sa nyid du sbyar byas la// klu rnams thams cad 'bed par
53b8(rgyud): 'gyur// lag pa g.yon pa la 'khor lo 'di dngos su 'am yid kyis bris la sngags// len gcig bzlas pas bya bas na// 'dre bdug gis zin pa spong babyed de/
54a1(rgyud): #ka ra bi ra'i dastug gu dris te// lan cig bzlas rlig na mngal gang du 'phro bar 'dod pa der 'pho bar 'gyur ro// dug dang lan tshwa dang ske chos dris te/
54a2(rgyud): khros na gsod par 'gyur ro// ro bsregs pa'i 'ga' ba da du ri'i khu bas me bsad de/ 'byung po'i nyi ma la de nyid kyis 'khor lo dris la// lan cig bzlas
54a3(rgyud): pas de gang la bsnun pa de ltung bar 'gyur ro// sang ka ti'i gastag gus sngags pas cho ga snga ma bzhin bris la// thal ba la mngon par sngags te// gang la snun pa de
54a4(rgyud): sha dzas bzung bar 'gyur ro// dur khrod kyi sol bas shin leb bam rtsi ga ngos la/ 'byung po'i mtshan ma gang gi snying khar bris pa de// don chen pos bzung bar 'gyuraro//
54a5(rgyud): bsgrub bya'i gzugs bcug la/ de'i snying khar 'khrul 'khor bcug ste// zhag bdun gyi bar du dri'i chu'i nang du bzhag nas// a ti mug la'i lcug ma la lan bdun
54a6(rgyud): sngags ste de la bsnun na zhag bdun gyi mthar rlung gi shugs kyis 'ong bar 'gyur ro// 'khor lo de nyid bye drag du dur khrod kyi sar la// pho nya'i kha dog gis bye brag du
54a7(rgyud): gyur pa dris la// las kyi pho nya dang lhan cig du sgrub par bya'o// ka ra bi ri'i lcug ma khru phyed dang gnyis kyi tshang dang ldan pas// gang la mngon par phyogs te sngags
54a8(rgyud): bris nas/ ro bsregs pa'i me 'bar ba la dor te// ji srid mtshig par myur du drangs la// rig pa'i rgyal po lan bdun bzlas nas// gang zhig dran de klang la
54b1(rgyud): bskor na// de de'i mod la rlung gi shugs kyis 'ong bar 'gyur ro// skyes pa'i ro'i kham phor la// dab la dang yung ba'i khu bas gang gi ming dris pa de de'i mod/
54b2(rgyud): la bcings par 'gyuraro// dur khrod kyi ser sa pa rtswa mtshan gyi ras lo// shing a sho ka'i bstug gus// klu rnams spangs pa'i 'khor lo 'di bris la//
54b3(rgyud): de'i dbus su sngags pas cho ga bzhin yi ge e dang spel ba bris na/ mkha'agro ma'i khyad par thams cad dang / lus srul po thams bcings par 'gyur/
54b4(rgyud): zod pa la skyes pa'i khrag khrig gis gang gis ming bris la/ sngags pa khro ba dang bcas pas sngags bzlas na/ de'i khrag 'gugs par byed la// yid zhib dang /
54b5(rgyud): ldan pas sngags bzlas na/ slar gtong bar 'gyur ro// 'khor lo de nyid zla bas brgyan cing gsal ba// go ro tsa nas gro ga la skar ma rgyal gyi nyin bris te// bud med
54b6(rgyud): gang gi rtag tu bcangs na// rig pa'i rgyal po de nyid de'i lhum su 'jug par 'gyur ro// bud med dang zhi ba'i 'dus pa'i kun tu spyod pa'i mi'i mchog de'i lag
54b7(rgyud): mthil na yod pa'i dpal gang gis kyang 'phrog par mi nus la/ rnam pa de lta bu'i mchog dang ldan pas ni/ dngos grub thams cad kyi 'bras bu ster bar 'gyur/
54b8(rgyud): bcom ldan pa 'das 'di la ni/ brtul zhugs dang spyod pa dang bsnyung ba dang cho ga med par yang // cho ga zhib mo'i sbyor ba'i tshul 'di nyid kyis/ las thams cad ji
55a1(rgyud): #/ ltar 'dod pa bzhin byed do// nam mkha'i dbyings kyi dbus bsam pa// zla ba'i dkyil 'khor dam pa ste// 'od zer tshogs ni gsal ba'i mngangs/
55a2(rgyud): 'khor lo'i phreng bas rnam par klubs// de dbus 'khor lo rtsibs brgyad dang // pad+ma'i phreng ba shin du mdzes// slar yang 'khor lo bri bar bya// rdo rje phreng ba rnam
55a3(rgyud): par phro// ska gsung thugs kyi rdo rje yi// dkyil 'khor dkyil 'khor lta bu yin/ na mkha' thams cad g.yo byed pa// rang gi lus la spro bar bya// dkar dang mar dang
55a4(rgyud): sngo ba ste// kha dog mchog gis bye brag bya// bu'i cho ga 'di yis ni// dpa' bo'i dbang phyug de bzhin bri// dbus su bsgrub par bya ba'i ming // ji ltar 'dod bzhin sbyar bar bya//
55a5(rgyud): rdol rdo rje phreng ba ni// 'od zer 'bar ba'i phreng 'khrugs bri// 'di ni bsrung ba chen mo ste/ thams cad bsrung ba bla na med/ rim dang nang dang dug dang ni/ mkha' 'gro ma yis 'tshe
55a6(rgyud): ba dang / gdon dang bdud dang log 'dren dang / gang yang lus srul la sogs pa/ grib ma yang ni mi gom na/ de'i lus lta smos ci dgos/ zla gzugs lta bu'i yi ge lta/
55a7(rgyud): phyogs bcur rnam par 'byed par byed// dkar po yis ni zhi 'gyur te/ nag po skra cig dag gis bsod// dmar po yis ni dbang byed do// de nyid kyis ni nges par 'gugs/ ser
55a8(rgyud): bos nges par 'ching 'gyur te/ dmag gi dpung ni 'ching bar 'gyur// zhes bcom ldan 'das kyis gsungs te/ las thams cad 'byung ba zhes bya ba'i bsrung 'khor la'o//
55b1(rgyud): bka' yi 'khor lo'i khyad par ni/ de nas yang dag bshad par bya// las kyi cho ga mthong ba yis// sems kun don byed pa'o// nam mkha' dbyings kyi dbus gnas par//
55b2(rgyud): zla ba'i dkyil 'khor lta bu yi// dkyil 'khor dkyil 'khor lta bur bsam/ bcu drug 'dab mas rnam par brgyan// de dbus pad chen 'dab brgyad pa// rdo rje rtse lnga pa'i ya mchog/
55b3(rgyud): 'od zer dkar pos shin du mdzes// sgrub pos 'khor lo'i phyi rol du// pad ma'i lte bar swa hA dri// dngos grub thams cad ltar ba'o// ma mo'i khyim ni nyams dga' bar// tsan dan
55b4(rgyud): dmar pos byubs nas ni// 'dol zhing shin tu 'jam pa'i// stan la skye gnas phyag rgya bcings// sngags pas bsgrub bya mngon phyogs te/ brgya rtsa brgyad du bzlas par bya// yan
55b5(rgyud): lag rus pas brgyan bsam zhing // gcer bur gyur pas rang gis bri/ yi dgas gos sam ro yis ni// bum pa skam po dag la yang / yi dgas sems can rtsi khrag dang /

55b8(rgyud): 'dag ma du med la// blo dang ldan pas nyin bdun bsro// sgrub po yis brgya bzlas nas/ rgyal po blon bcas 'dun na 'don/ btsun mo'i 'khor dang bcas par ni// myur du 'gugs
56a1(rgyud): #par byed pa yin// gro ga yi ni 'dab ma la// ro yis sen rtsi ro rtsa nas// ma'i bdag po 'khor sa bcas pa// ming dang spel te bri bar bya// mngon par phyogs

101'b2(rgyud): ma dang // skar ma rgyal dang ldan pa la/ mchod dang gtor mi'icho ga yis// shin tu mnyam par bzhag pas bzung / khyu mchog rA yis dang ni// phyi nas gcig tu bsre bar bya//
101'b3(rgyud): lo gcig par du nus dang ldan// de nas sar pa gzhan bzung bya// ji srid lus la gnas kyi bar// mtshon chas chod cing phugs ma 'gyur// sgrub po de yi lus la ni// dug kyang 'pho/
101'b4(rgyud): bar mi 'gyur ro// sngar bstan cho ga bya ba yis// b+h+ra ma dan ta'i sman bzung bya// pad ma yi ni 'dam dang ni// lhan gcig tu ni bsre bar bya// sngar bstan cho ga'i rim pa yis//
101'b5(rgyud): i sha ri ni bzung bar bya// mtshon ma gcig gi se dag dang // shin tu mnyam par bzhag ste bsre// yon tan dag ni spre ma bzhin// nyon cig lha mo shes rab che// ku ma ri
101'b6(rgyud): zhes bya ba'i sman// gzhon nu ma yi rkang rjes rdul// de yi gci ba'i sa dang bcas// ma he'i ri yis dang ldan// 'dam 'di sum bcu gsum pas mchod/ de nas yang dag

103b7(rgyud): du bzlas pa'i chus/ der ni bcu ste bskyed par bya// gzhan du yid btag 'tshe ba 'byung // 'bu la sogs pa bsrung ba dang // shing bskyed rig byed bzhin du bya// ni 'bad
